This means that I have a dedicated account strategist who assists with outreach, program management, troubleshooting, and more. The service provided has always been above par and it's one of the easiest platforms to work in. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">The reporting is challenging to work in, sometimes. For immediate tracking (7 days, last month, etc.), it's straightforward to get the reporting I need, but if I need something in a larger time frame (say a three-year history), I have to reach out to my account strategist because the reporting platform will time out. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-5212830 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Partnerize allows our eCommerce business to scale sales aggressively while being able to control costs and keep them within a confirmed budget. d="M13.333 0L6.667 6.667l-4-4L0 5.333 6.667 12 16 2.667z"></path></svg></div></div><div class="tag" data-container="body" title="Invitation from a seller or affiliate. This reviewer was not provided any incentive by G2 for completing this review." ue="tooltip">Review source: Seller invite</div></div></div><div class="paper__bd"><div class="d-f mb-1"><div class="f-1 d-f ai-c mb-half-small-only"><div class="stars large xlarge--medium-down stars-8"></div><div class="time-stamp pl-4th ws-nw"><span><span class="x-current-review-date" data-poison-date=""><meta content="2022-02-20" itemprop="datePublished"><time datetime="2022-02-20">Feb 20, 2022</time></span></span></div></div></div><div class="d-f"><div class="f-1"><div data-poison=""><a class="pjax" href="https://www.g2.com/products/partnerize/reviews/partnerize-review-5361475"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Useful, valuable, user-friendly but most importantly accurate."</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Of all the affiliate software, Partnerize is among the best when it comes to accuracy and flexibility.  There are quite a few beneficial reports that you can't find elsewhere and they really provide a nice set of options to choose from. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">What appears as a dislike is more of a "less bad" scenario. There is no question that Partnerize software is among the best in the affiliate industry but it is definitely a necessary evil. They don't like to be called an "affiliate network" but rather a SaaS. To each, their own but they seem to make an extraordinary effort to avoid the "affiliate network" connotation. They serve the affiliate industry more than any other it would seem and it's an insult to many of those they serve in the affiliate industry if they are too good for such a title. Are they too good to use such a title? More importantly, then what they will or won't allow themselves to be called is that as a SaaS they escape the necessity to service publishers on the front end and instead push us off to contact the company for help. It's really annoying when we spend the time to send our issue to the company who built the system, who one would think would know how to fix an issue but instead, we have to send it elsewhere to someone who may not have any idea to fix which would require us to go back to Partnerize anyhow. This only wastes everyone's time. I raise this here because it has happened more times than I care to admit. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-5361475 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">Recommendations to others considering Partnerize:</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Manage your expectations. The information is there and is good but it will take you a long time to figure out how to find what you need and you are not going to get much assistance from the internal staff. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-5361475 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Partnerize allows us to integrate and grow our relationships with many more merchants than if we weren't connected. We have been able to earn additional revenue and develop new partnerships with advertisers in other regions of the world. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized" ue="toggle-class login-modal-toggle" Their analytics capabilities are exceptional, so you can always get deep insights into the success of your program in no time at all. They are constantly introducing valuable new capabilities across their entire platform. It's truly an all-in-one platform that has amazing capabilities. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I wish that they developed more strict requirements for vetting new partners before allowing them onto the platform. While they have a tremendous amount of high-quality partners, there's a lot of inferior ones too. They also need to put controls in place that stop potential partners from repeatedly contacting you to request to join your campaign. I'm very hopeful they will address these pain points soon. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4777083 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">We're trying to drive incremental growth for our subscription business at a low CPA. Additionally, we are trying to diversify our channel mix and not be so reliant on channels such as paid search. Partnerize has allowed us to do precisely that, and we're just getting started. I'm really looking forward to continuing to grow and evolve our program in partnership with them. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div href="https://www.g2.com/products/partnerize/reviews/partnerize-review-4151086"><div class="m-0 l2" itemprop="name">"Robust and innovative affiliate tech solution backed by great people."</div></a></div><div data-poison-text=""><div itemprop="reviewBody"><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you like best about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Partnerize provides its users the ability to manage all types partnerships in-house, whether they're traditional cost-per-action agreements or bespoke brand partnerships. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">I dislike that I don't yet fully harness the complete range of platform capabilities due to a lack of internal resource. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4151086 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">Recommendations to others considering Partnerize:</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Partnerize is a great platform backed by a group of smart and helpful people. I'd recommend Partnerize to any business considering bringing their affiliate and partnership program in-house. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4151086 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Ensuring all relevant partner contacts are receiving communications. This was difficult to manage in the past however the platform's Communication Tool has evolved and can now reach various email addresses. We now benefit from improved and more efficient communication lines with partners.</p><p class="formatted-text"></p><p class="formatted-text">The Affiliate channel has always been a consistent performer that we depend on for generating sales from our traditional mix of affiliates. Whilst we achieve a constant flow of traffic and revenue, finding that next new partnership to grow the channel can often be difficult when juggling every other task on the plate. Working closely with Partnerize's Customer Success team to utilise their Partner Discovery tool has allowed us to easily find new suitable partners, as well as making SurfStitch's campaign more visible and accessible than ever. It really saves me a lot of time and effort when trying to grow the channel and our breadth of partners. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div They also take the time to connect you with partners on their platform but also introduce partnerships that not your average affiliate partnership. They take the connection past the platform and into the industry through brand to brand introductions as well as recommendations on who to work with on the platform. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div><div class="l5 mt-2">What do you dislike about Partnerize?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Sometimes it can be very time consuming to connect with a new partner via the platform and then onboard with that partner. Another thing is that a few partners will be categorised under their operating country, i.e. UK or US, but also have an audience in AUS... Unfortunately you won't know that until you have a conversation with that partner. It would be nice to have a "media" kit on audience size in each country they are active in. It would also be nice to have a function that identifies and recommends similar partners to the one's that you are seeing a lot of success/conversions from. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4642036 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">Recommendations to others considering Partnerize:</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Partnerize is there to support you with your needs and objectives. Have an open conversation with them on what you are trying to achieve and they will provide their recommendations and connections tailored to you. There is always an opportunity to learn more from their webinars and networking sessions. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div><div class="expanded-review-4642036 is-hidden-default"><div class="l5 mt-2">What problems is Partnerize solving and how is that benefiting you?</div><div><p class="formatted-text">Working with Partnerize has opened up opportunities with digital partners that would not work with until now. We are able to have one pixel on our site and connect with multiple partners by sending a report to them via the Partnerize platform. <span class="spht">Review collected by and hosted on G2.com.</span></p></div></div></div><div class="flex justify-between"><a class="link d-f ai-c x-show-more js-log-click x-toggle-class-initialized" ue="toggle-class login-modal-toggle"
